# First Lacerda Event
country_event = {
	id = brazil_lacerda.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_lacerda.1" }
	title = brazil_lacerda.1.t
	desc = brazil_lacerda.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_lacerda_intro

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = brazil_lacerda.1.a
		BRA_develop_decrease_highway_speed_2 = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = paternalism } }
			country_event = {
				id = brazil_lacerda.2
			}
		}
	}
}

				type = infrastructure

				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		BRA_decrease_UDN_management_x_by_50 = yes
		BRA_decrease_UDN_management_y_by_25 = yes
	}

		name = brazil_lacerda.11.b

			}

country_event = { ## Healthcare Law Passes
	id = brazil_lacerda.34
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_lacerda.34" }
	title = brazil_lacerda.34.t
	desc = brazil_lacerda.34.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_women_in_congress

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = brazil_lacerda.34.a
		BRA_boost_UDN_candidates_nationwide_med = yes
		TNO_improve_healthcare_med = yes
		TNO_improve_health_care_policy_effectiveness_high = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = BRA_rely_on_market }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = tno_health_care_support_for_emergencies
				add_idea = tno_health_care_low_income_protections
			}
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = tno_health_care_support_for_emergencies
				add_idea = tno_health_care_universal_health_care

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #
		name = brazil_lacerda.185.a

			add_political_power = 50
			add_stability = 0.05
			army_experience = 50
			admin_funding_maximal_increase_low = yes
			admin_funding_minimal_increase_low = yes
			TNO_improve_army_professionalism_low = yes
			TNO_improve_security_policy_effectiveness_med = yes
			TNO_improve_penal_system_policy_effectiveness_med = yes
			TNO_improve_training_policy_effectiveness_low = yes
			TNO_improve_military_supervision_policy_effectiveness_low = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_anti_riot_bill_success_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { temp_bill = token:BRA_ANTI_RIOT_BILL }
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.0 }
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_psd_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.2 }
			BRA_lacerda_calculate_udn_bill_support = yes
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.3 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_psp_support_flag }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill < BRA_lacerda_psp_support } }
					set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = BRA_lacerda_psp_support }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { BRA_lacerda_psp_support = 0 } }
					set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = BRA_lacerda_psp_support }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_prp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.2 }
			BRA_initialize_bill = yes
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_vote_days@var:temp_bill = 35 }
			BRA_call_bill_vote = yes
		}
	}
}

		add_political_power = -30
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_pl_immigration_repeal_bill_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { temp_bill = token:BRA_LACERDA_REPEAL_OF_JAPANESE_IMMIGRATION_BAN }
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.3 }
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_psd_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.45 }
			BRA_lacerda_calculate_udn_bill_support = yes
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.3 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_psp_support_flag }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill < BRA_lacerda_psp_support } }
					set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = BRA_lacerda_psp_support }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { BRA_lacerda_psp_support = 0 } }
					set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = BRA_lacerda_psp_support }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_prp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.5 }
			BRA_initialize_bill = yes
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_vote_days@var:temp_bill = 35 }
			BRA_call_bill_vote = yes
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_government = paternalism } }
				country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda.193 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

			multiply_temp_variable = { psp_amnt = BRA_pl_psp_support_pct }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_pct = psp_amnt }

			set_temp_variable = { prp_amnt = global.SA_tension }
			divide_temp_variable = { prp_amnt = 100 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { prp_amnt = BRA_pl_prp_support_pct }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pl_prp_support_pct = prp_amnt }
			BRA_update_pl = yes
		}
	}
}

		}

			limit = { check_variable = { BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_unity > 75 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = brazil_lacerda_strikes.9.tt
			set_variable = { BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_unity = 75 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = BRA_70_braga_candidate
				}
			}

				id = brazil_lacerda_strikes.10
				days = 3
			}
		}

			country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_world_tour.1 days = 30 }
			set_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_world_tour
		}
	}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_lacerda_strikes.18" }
	title = brazil_lacerda_strikes.18.t
	desc = brazil_lacerda_strikes.18.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_court_case_2
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = BRA_Riots_tavora_negotiations_collapse
		}
		has_country_flag = BRA_Riots_Show_GUI
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = brazil_lacerda_strikes.18.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_Riots_CGT_warning_tt
		set_country_flag = BRA_Riots_CGT_warning
		set_temp_variable = { BRA_Riots_CGT_Radicalism_Temp = -20 }
		BRA_Riots_CGT_Radicalism_Change = yes
	}
}

country_event = { ## Lacerda wins without comprimising
	id = brazil_lacerda_strikes.26
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_lacerda_strikes.26" }
	title = brazil_lacerda_strikes.26.t
	desc = brazil_lacerda_strikes.26.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_lacerda_crow

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = brazil_lacerda_strikes.26.a
		set_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_strikes_over
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_lacerda_success_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_coup_happened
					has_country_flag = BRA_sorbonne_lacerda
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_imp.5 days = 3 }
			hidden_effect = { remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = BRA_lacerda_strikes_dynmod } }
		}
		else = {
			remove_ideas = BRA_general_strke_lacerda
			hidden_effect = {
				BRA_Carlos_Lacerda = {
					promote_character = {
						ideology = conservatism_free_market_conservatism_subtype
					}
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = conservatism
					long_name = BRA_conservatism_2_party_long
					name = BRA_conservatism_2_party
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = BRA_lacerda_strikes_dynmod }
				set_temp_variable = { temp = party_popularity@liberal_conservatism }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = conservatism
					popularity = temp
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = { temp = -1 }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = liberal_conservatism
					popularity = temp
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = conservatism
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

## Samba events
country_event = { # max economic liberalism event
	id = brazil_lacerda_samba.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_lacerda_samba.1" }
	title = brazil_lacerda_samba.1.t
	desc = brazil_lacerda_samba.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_lacerda_samba

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = brazil_lacerda_samba.1.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = brazil_lacerda_samba.1.tt
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { TNO_economy_type = token:Econ_Type_Capitalism } } }
			set_temp_variable = { TNO_economy_type_temp = token:Econ_Type_Capitalism }
			econ_type_change = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { interest_rates_temp = -1.25 }
			econ_interest_rates_change = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { inflation_temp = -3 }
		econ_inflation_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = -2.5 }
		econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { econ_centralization_temp = -25 }
		econ_centralization_change = yes
		TNO_worsen_minimum_wage_policy_effectiveness_high = yes
		TNO_worsen_income_taxation_policy_effectiveness_med = yes
		add_ideas = BRA_lacerdas_dream
		custom_effect_tooltip = brazil_lacerda_samba.1.tt2
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		BRA = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = BRA_Carlos_Lacerda
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_government = paternalism }
	}
	option = { #
		name = brazil_lacerda_samba.42.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { BRA_lacerda_udn_bossa_quarter = yes }
				country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_samba.43 days = 14 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { BRA_lacerda_udn_realistas_quarter = yes }
				country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_samba.44 days = 14 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { BRA_lacerda_udn_banda_quarter = yes }
				country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_samba.45 days = 14 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { BRA_lacerda_udn_party_balanced = yes }
				country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_samba.45 days = 14 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { BRA_lacerda_udn_liberais_quarter = yes }
				country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_samba.46 days = 14 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #
	id = brazil_lacerda_samba.46
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_lacerda_samba.46" }
	title = brazil_lacerda_samba.46.t
	desc = brazil_lacerda_samba.46.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_campos

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #work with PTB
		name = brazil_lacerda_samba.46.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_pl_hydroelectric_bill_tooltip
		effect_tooltip = {
			497 = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = thermoelectric_plant
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			499 = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = thermoelectric_plant
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { temp_bill = token:BRA_LACERDA_HYDROELECTRIC_BILL }
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.6 }
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_psd_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.3 }
			BRA_lacerda_calculate_udn_bill_support = yes
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.4 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_psp_support_flag }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill < BRA_lacerda_psp_support } }
					set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = BRA_lacerda_psp_support }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { BRA_lacerda_psp_support = 0 } }
					set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = BRA_lacerda_psp_support }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_prp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.3 }
			BRA_initialize_bill = yes
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_vote_days@var:temp_bill = 28 }
			BRA_call_bill_vote = yes
			set_country_flag = dam_bill_ptb_support
		}
	}
	option = { #negotiate with lacerda
		name = brazil_lacerda_samba.46.b
		add_political_power = -50
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_pl_hydroelectric_bill_tooltip
		effect_tooltip = {
			497 = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = thermoelectric_plant
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			499 = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = thermoelectric_plant
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { temp_bill = token:BRA_LACERDA_HYDROELECTRIC_BILL }
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.0 }
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_psd_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.2 }
			BRA_lacerda_calculate_udn_bill_support = yes
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.3 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_psp_support_flag }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill < BRA_lacerda_psp_support } }
					set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = BRA_lacerda_psp_support }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { BRA_lacerda_psp_support = 0 } }
					set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = BRA_lacerda_psp_support }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_prp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.2 }
			BRA_initialize_bill = yes
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_vote_days@var:temp_bill = 28 }
			BRA_call_bill_vote = yes
		}
	}
	option = { #threaten lacerda with resignation
		name = brazil_lacerda_samba.46.c
		add_political_power = -100
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_pl_hydroelectric_bill_tooltip

				}

					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}

					level = 1

				}
			}
			1490 = {

					type = thermoelectric_plant
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}

			set_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.1 }
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_psd_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.3 }
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_udn_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 1 }
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.3 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_psp_support_flag }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill < BRA_lacerda_psp_support } }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #
		name = brazil_lacerda_samba.62.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { temp_bill = token:BRA_LACERDA_NATIONAL_SECURITY_LAWS_REFORM }
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.05 }
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_psd_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.1 }
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_udn_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.6 }
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.05 }
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_prp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.1 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { BRA_national_security_acts_counter = 0 } } }
				multiply_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_support_bill@var:temp_bill = BRA_national_security_acts_counter }
				multiply_variable = { BRA_pl_psd_support_bill@var:temp_bill = BRA_national_security_acts_counter }
				multiply_variable = { BRA_pl_udn_support_bill@var:temp_bill = BRA_national_security_acts_counter }
				multiply_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = BRA_national_security_acts_counter }
				multiply_variable = { BRA_pl_prp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = BRA_national_security_acts_counter }
			}
			BRA_initialize_bill = yes
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_vote_days@var:temp_bill = 28 }
			BRA_call_bill_vote = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_pl_lacerda_security_acts_bill_tooltip
	}
}

country_event = { #full success
	id = brazil_lacerda_samba.63
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_lacerda_samba.63" }
	title = brazil_lacerda_samba.63.t
	desc = brazil_lacerda_samba.63.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_campos

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #
		name = brazil_lacerda_samba.63.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = BRA_lott_act_passed_flag }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_law = token:BRA_the_lott_act_law }
			TNO_remove_assorted_law = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = { BRA_national_security_act_law_var = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_lacerda_security_acts_success
		BRA_military_increase_loyalty_high = yes
		# setting const power to 5
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_lacerda_acts_const_purge
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { temp_const = BRA_military_const_power }
			set_variable = { BRA_military_const_power = 5 }
			divide_temp_variable = { temp_const = 2 }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_military_sorbonne_power = temp_const }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_military_hardliners_power = temp_const }
			BRA_military_update = yes
		}
		#
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = BRA
			popularity = -0.03
		}
		set_temp_variable = { temp_tick_x = 5 }
		BRA_UDN_change_x_tick = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_udn_unity = 6 }
		BRA_lacerda_udn_unity_change = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = BRA_sec_acts_adhemar }
			BRA_military_increase_nepotism_high = yes
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = BRA_65_lacerda_presidency }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = paternalism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = paternalism_1
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #
		name = brazil_lacerda_samba.66.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { #const dominant
					AND = {
						check_variable = {
							var = BRA_military_const_power
							value = BRA_military_hardliners_power
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
						check_variable = {
							var = BRA_military_const_power
							value = BRA_military_sorbonne_power
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_samba.54 days = 14 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { #hardliners dominant
					AND = {
						check_variable = {
							var = BRA_military_hardliners_power
							value = BRA_military_const_power
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
						check_variable = {
							var = BRA_military_hardliners_power
							value = BRA_military_sorbonne_power
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_samba.56 days = 14 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { #sorbonne dominant
					AND = {
						check_variable = {
							var = BRA_military_sorbonne_power
							value = BRA_military_const_power
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
						check_variable = {
							var = BRA_military_sorbonne_power
							value = BRA_military_hardliners_power
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_samba.55 days = 14 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #ask the army for help
		name = brazil_lacerda_samba.77.a
		hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { BRA_military_hardliners_power < 30 } }
			country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_samba.78 days = 14 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = BRA_military_hardliners_power
					value = 30
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = BRA_lott_act_passed_flag }
				country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_samba.79 days = 14 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_samba.80 days = 14 }
			}
		}
		}
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		AND = {
			BRA = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = BRA_Carlos_Lacerda
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = BRA_lacerda_coup_happened
					has_country_flag = BRA_sorbonne_lacerda
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #conservative program gets adopted
		name = brazil_lacerda_samba.81.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_pol
				value = 50
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		#small boost for magalhaes election
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_samba.82 days = 180 }
		}
	}
	option = { #compromise program gets adopted
		name = brazil_lacerda_samba.81.b
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_pol < 50 }
				check_variable = { BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_pol > -50 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_samba.82 days = 180 }
		}
	}
	option = { #radical program gets adopted
		name = brazil_lacerda_samba.81.c
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = BRA_lacerda_udn_manage_pol
				value = -50
				compare = less_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		#small harm for magalhaes election
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_samba.82 days = 180 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = brazil_oc_tavora.1
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_oc_tavora.1"
	}
	title = brazil_oc_tavora.1.t
	desc = brazil_oc_tavora.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_crise_petrolifera

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = brazil_oc_tavora.1.a
		hidden_effect = { add_ideas = BRA_fight_thrifty }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.1 }
		econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
		army_funding_maximal_decrease_high = yes
		add_war_support = -0.05
		army_funding_minimal_increase_high = yes
		naval_funding_minimal_increase_high = yes
		nuclear_funding_minimal_increase_high = yes
		add_to_variable = { BRA_crise_petrolifera_org_loss = 0.05 }
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = train_tech
			bonus = 0.5
			uses = 1
			category = train_tech
		}

		country_event = {
			id = brazil_oc_tavora.2
			days = 14
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = brazil_lacerda_sorbonne_campaign.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_lacerda_sorbonne_campaign.3" }
	title = brazil_lacerda_sorbonne_campaign.3.t
	desc = brazil_lacerda_sorbonne_campaign.3.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_lacerda_generic_1

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = brazil_lacerda_sorbonne_campaign.3.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = brazil_lacerda_sorbonne_campaign.3.tt
		for_loop_effect = {
			end = BRA_pres_candidates^num
			value = i
			break = break
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { BRA_pres_candidates^i = 9 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { braga_index = i }
				set_temp_variable = { break = 1 }
			}
		}
		for_loop_effect = {
			end = 9
			value = region_id
			set_temp_variable = { idx = region_id }
			multiply_temp_variable = { idx = BRA_pres_candidates^num }
			add_to_temp_variable = { idx = braga_index }
			set_temp_variable = { amount = -150000 }
			divide_temp_variable = { amount = BRA_pres_region_pop^region_id }
			multiply_temp_variable = { amount = BRA_pres_infra^idx }
			multiply_temp_variable = { amount = BRA_pres_fatigue^region_id }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^idx = amount }
			custom_effect_tooltip = brazil_lacerda_sorbonne_campaign.3.a.tt
		}
		BRA_redraw_pres_info = yes
		BRA_pres_select_region = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = BRA_keep_an_eye_on_things }
				country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_sorbonne_campaign.5 days = 10 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_sorbonne_campaign.6 days = 10 }
			}
		}
	}
}

			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^idx = amount }

		}

country_event = {
	id = brazil_lacerda_sorbonne_campaign.28
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_lacerda_sorbonne_campaign.28" }
	title = brazil_lacerda_sorbonne_campaign.28.t
	desc = brazil_lacerda_sorbonne_campaign.28.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_kubitschek_car

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = brazil_lacerda_sorbonne_campaign.28.a
		add_political_power = 15
		for_loop_effect = {
			end = BRA_pres_candidates^num
			value = i
			break = break
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { BRA_pres_candidates^i = 9 }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { braga_index = i }
				set_temp_variable = { break = 1 }
			}
		}
		for_loop_effect = {
			end = 9
			value = region_id
			set_temp_variable = { idx = region_id }
			multiply_temp_variable = { idx = BRA_pres_candidates^num }
			add_to_temp_variable = { idx = braga_index }
			set_temp_variable = { amount = 300000 }
			divide_temp_variable = { amount = BRA_pres_region_pop^region_id }
			multiply_temp_variable = { amount = BRA_pres_infra^idx }
			multiply_temp_variable = { amount = BRA_pres_fatigue^region_id }
			add_to_variable = { BRA_pres_support^idx = amount }
			custom_effect_tooltip = brazil_lacerda_sorbonne_campaign.28.tt
		}
		BRA_redraw_pres_info = yes
		BRA_pres_select_region = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_sorbonne_campaign.31 days = 10 }
		}
	}
}

				limit = { check_variable = { BRA_lacerda_campaign_success = -2 } }
				country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_campaign.39 days = 7 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = brazil_lacerda_campaign.38 days = 7 }
			}
		}
	}
}
